	    "RequiresTier"              "1"
		
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"			"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"health_restored"	"225"
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"			"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"duration"   		"45"
			}
			"03"

				"var_type"			"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"radius"			"600"
			}
	        "04"
	        {
	            "var_type"          "FIELD_INTEGER"
	            "health_per_second" "5"
	        }
		}
	
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"FireEffect"
			{
				"Target" 			"CASTER"

			}

			"ApplyModifier"
			{
				"ModifierName"	"modifier_scroll_of_regeneration"

				}
				"Duration"		"%duration"
			}			
			"FireSound"
			{
				"EffectName"	"DOTA_Item.Mekansm.Activate"
				"Target" 		"CASTER"
			}
	
			"SpendCharge"
			{}
		}
	
		"Modifiers"
		{

			{

	            "TextureName"       "item_scroll_of_regeneration"
		
				"Properties"

				}

						"ModifierName"	"modifier_scroll_of_regeneration"

				}
			}
		}

	   	"BaseClass" 					"item_datadriven"
